### Implementation Notes for Developers
#### Screen-to-Table Mapping

| Screen | Primary Tables                                                                   | Key Fields
|--------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------
| SC-01	 | hpc_templates, hpc_template_parts, hpc_template_sections, hpc_template_rubrics	| All template structure fields
| SC-02	 | hpc_circular_goals, hpc_circular_goal_competency_jnt	| goal details, competency mappings
| SC-03	 | hpc_learning_outcomes, hpc_outcome_entity_jnt, hpc_outcome_question_jnt	| outcome details, topic mappings
| SC-05	 | hpc_reports, slb_students, attendance_students	| student list, report status
| SC-06	 | hpc_report_items (with rubric mapping to Part-A)	| student demographics
| SC-08	 | hpc_student_evaluation, hpc_report_items	| domain assessments
| SC-09	 | hpc_learning_activities, hpc_student_evaluation	| activity assessments
| SC-10	 | hpc_report_items	| teacher feedback
